The Company posted quarterly revenue of $95.4 billion, up 5 percent year over year, and quarterly diluted earnings per share of $1.65, up 8 percent year over year.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Helvetica',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;Today Apple is reporting strong quarterly results, including double-digit growth in Services,&#8221; said Tim Cook, Apple&#8217;s CEO. &#8220;We were happy to welcome iPhone 16e to our lineup, and to introduce powerful new Macs and iPads that take advantage of the extraordinary capabilities of Apple silicon. And we were proud to announce that we&#8217;ve cut our carbon emissions by 60 percent over the past decade.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Helvetica',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;Our March quarter business performance drove EPS growth of 8 percent and $24 billion in operating cash flow, allowing us to return $29 billion to shareholders,&#8221; said Kevan Parekh, Apple&#8217;s CFO. &#8220;And thanks to our high levels of customer loyalty and satisfaction, our installed base of active devices once again reached a new all-time high across all product categories and geographic segments.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Helvetica',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Apple&#8217;s board of directors has declared a cash dividend of $0.26 per share of the Company&#8217;s common stock, an increase of 4 percent. The dividend is payable on May 15, 2025 to shareholders of record as of the close of business on May 12, 2025. The board of directors has also authorized an additional program to repurchase up to $100 billion of the Company&#8217;s common stock.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Helvetica',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Apple will provide live streaming of its Q2 2025 financial results conference call beginning at 2&#58;00 p.m. PT on May 1, 2025 at apple.com&#47;investor&#47;earnings-call.
